#######################  Uniform Factories  ##########################
country_event = {
	id = uniformfactory.1
	title = uniformfactory.1.t
	desc = uniformfactory.1.d # instructions on uniforms factories
	
	picture = GFX_event_uniform_producer

	trigger = {
		date > 1936.1.1
		uniform_factory > 0
		uniform_factory < 2
		NOT = { has_country_flag = uniformfactory_update }
		NOT = { has_idea = uniformfactory1 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
        days = 2
    }
	
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = uniformfactory_update }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory2 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory3 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory4 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory5 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory6 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory7 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory8 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory9 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory10 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory11 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory12 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory13 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory14 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory15 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory16 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory17 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory18 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory19 }
		hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = uniformfactory20 }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = uniformfactory0 }
	}

	option = {
		name = uniformfactory.1.a
		add_ideas = uniformfactory1
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = uniformfactory_update }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ltaircraftfactory.1
	title = ltaircraftfactory.1.t
	desc = ltaircraftfactory.1.d # instructions on ltaircrafts factories
	
	picture = GFX_event_aircraft_producer

	trigger = {
    NOT = { tag = GER }
    NOT = { tag = JAP }
    NOT = { tag = SOV }

        NOT = { has_idea = ltaircraftfactory1 }

		date > 1936.1.1
		ltaircraft_factory > 0
		ltaircraft_factory < 2
		NOT = { has_country_flag = ltaircraftfactory_update }
	}

        days = 2
    }
	   immediate = { 
	   hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = ltaircraftfactory_update }
	   hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory2 } 
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory3 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory4 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory5 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory6 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory7 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory8 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory9 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory10 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory11 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory12 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory13 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory14 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory15 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory16 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory17 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory18 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory19 }
		 hidden_effect = { remove_ideas = ltaircraftfactory20 }
		 hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = ltaircraftfactory0 }
	    }

	option = {
